***измельчить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:измельчить.html>измельчи́ть</a> (26085)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мельчи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">melʹčítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измельчить.html>измельчи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izmelʹčítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измельчать.html>измельча́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to crumble up, to chop, to crush, to pound, to grind
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:измельчить.html>измельчи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кора.html>кору́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izmelʹčítʹ</b> korú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to chop the bark</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:измельчить.html>измельчи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порошок.html>порошо́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izmelʹčítʹ</b> v porošók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to powder, reduce to powder</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***измена.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́на</a> (6240)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izména</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>betrayal, treason
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:государственный.html>госуда́рственная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́на</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:родина.html>Ро́дине</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gosudárstvennaja izména; izména Rodine</i> ― <span class="e-translation">high treason</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>unfaithfulness, faithlessness
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:супружеский.html>супру́жеская</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">suprúžeskaja izména</i> ― <span class="e-translation">unfaithfulness, (conjugal) infidelity</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предательство.html>преда́тельство</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">predátelʹstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">адюльте́р</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">adjulʹtɛ́r</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неверность.html>неве́рность</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nevérnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***изменить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изменить.html>измени́ть</a> (1733)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мѣнити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">měniti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*měniti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменить.html>измени́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izmenítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменять.html>изменя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to change, to alter, to modify, to edit</li>
<li>to vary</li>
<li><i>(with dative)</i> to betray, to become unfaithful, to cheat on</li>
<li>to break, to violate <i>(an oath, promise)</i></li>
<li>to fail <i>(memory)</i></li>
<li>to desert</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́на</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izména</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменение.html>измене́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izmenénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измениться.html>измени́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izmenítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменяться.html>изменя́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izmenjátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(intransitive)</i></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:менять.html>меня́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">menjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изменник.html>изме́нник</a> (10449)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izména</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменник.html>изме́нник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izménnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменник.html>изме́нника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменник.html>изме́нники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменник.html>изме́нников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изме́нница</b>)

<ol><li>traitor, betrayer</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предатель.html>преда́тель</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">predátelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ренегат.html>ренега́т</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">renegát</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***изменять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изменять.html>изменя́ть</a> (5902)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменить.html>измени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izmenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменять.html>изменя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izmenjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменить.html>измени́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to change, to alter, to modify, to edit</li>
<li>to vary</li>
<li><i>(with dative)</i> to betray, to become unfaithful</li>
<li>to break, to violate (an oath, promise)</li>
<li>to fail (memory)</li>
<li>to desert</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменение.html>измене́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izmenénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:измерение.html>измере́ние</a> (5701)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измерить.html>изме́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izméritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измерение.html>измере́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izmerénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измерение.html>измере́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измерение.html>измере́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измерение.html>измере́ний</a></b>)

<ol><li>measurement, measuring, gauging</li>
<li>dimension, size
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>трёх</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:измерение.html>измере́ниях</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v trjóx <b>izmerénijax</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">three-dimensional</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>тремя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:измерение.html>измере́ниями</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s tremjá <b>izmerénijami</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">three-dimensional</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>change, modification</li>
<li>survey</li>
<li>sounding, fathoming</li>
<li>determination</li></ol>

***измеряться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:измеряться.html>измеря́ться</a> (17844)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измеряться.html>изме́ряться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izmérjatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:измеряться.html>измеря́ться</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">изме́риться</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izméritʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измеряться.html>измеря́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izmerjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изме́риться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:измеряться.html>изме́ряться</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to measure <i>(a stated size)</i>, to amount <i>(to)</i>, to be as large [long, deep, etc] <i>(as)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́рево</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:измеряться.html>измеряется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тридцать.html>тридцатью́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:метр.html>ме́трами</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dérevo izmerjajetsja tridcatʹjú métrami</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the tree measures 30 metres</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запас.html>запа́сы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уголь.html>угля</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:измеряться.html>измеряются</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:миллион.html>миллио́нами</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тонна.html>то́нн</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zapásy uglja izmerjajutsja milliónami tonn</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the coal reserves amount to [are as large as] millions of tons</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измерять.html>измеря́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izmerjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***изможденный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изможденный.html>измождённый</a> (15384)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">измъжденъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izmŭždenŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, past passive participle of <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">измъждити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izmŭžditi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мозжи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mozžítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to ache dully but persistently</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мо́зглый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mózglyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dank; frail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, dialectal <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мо́згнуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mózgnutʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to spoil, to perish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мзга</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mzga</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wet weather</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изможденный.html>измождённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izmoždjónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>haggard, peaked</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изморозь.html>и́зморозь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ízmorozʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изморозь.html>и́зморози</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изморозь.html>и́зморози</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изморозь.html>и́зморозей</a></b>)

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>exhausted, worn out, tired out <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">experiencing exhaustion; of a person</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>exhausted, worn out, tired out <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">expressing exhaustion; of a face, look, tone, etc.; inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:измятый.html>измя́тый</a> (14303)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измятый.html>измя́тый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izmjátyj</span>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изнанка.html>изна́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iznánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изнанка.html>изна́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изнанка.html>изна́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изнанка.html>изна́нок</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изнасиловавший.html>изнаси́ловавший</a> (13761)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изнасиловавший.html>изнаси́ловавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iznasílovavšij</span>)
